<script type=text/javascript>

jQuery(document).ready(function() {	
 jQuery('#inv_results_container, #overview_content').on("click", "li img[src$='volkswagen.gif'], li img[src$='nonVWCertified.gif']", function (e){
		 e.stopPropagation()
		if(jQuery(this).attr('src').match(/volkswagen.gif$/)){
			var id = jQuery('#dialog-CPO');
		} else
			var id = jQuery('#dialog-QPO');
		
		//Get the screen height and width
		var maskHeight = jQuery(document).height();
		var maskWidth = jQuery(window).width();
	
		//Set heigth and width to mask to fill up the whole screen		
		if (jQuery.browser.msie){
			jQuery('.cblt-sneezeguard').css({'width':maskWidth,'height':maskHeight, 'top':'0px', 'left':'0px', 'display':'block'});
		} else {
			jQuery('.cblt-sneezeguard').css({'width':maskWidth,'height':maskHeight, 'top':'0px', 'left':'0px'});
		}
		
		//Sneezeguard transition effect		
		jQuery('.cblt-sneezeguard').fadeIn(500);	
	
		//Get the window height and width
		var winH = jQuery(window).height();
		var winW = jQuery(window).width();
              
		//Set the popup window to center
		jQuery(id).css('top',  winH/2-jQuery(id).height()/2);
		jQuery(id).css('left', winW/2-jQuery(id).width()/2);
	
		//modalWindow transition effect
		jQuery(id).fadeIn(500); 
	
	});
	
	//if close button is clicked
	jQuery('.modalWindow .modalClose').click(function (e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		jQuery('.cblt-sneezeguard').hide();
		jQuery('.modalWindow').hide();
	});		
	
	//if mask is clicked
	jQuery('.cblt-sneezeguard').click(function () {
		jQuery(this).hide();
		jQuery('.modalWindow').hide();
	});			
	
	// Esc Key closes modal popups
	jQuery(document).keyup(function(e) {
		if(e.keyCode == 27) {
			jQuery('.cblt-sneezeguard').hide();
			jQuery('.modalWindow').hide();
		}
	});

	jQuery(window).resize(function () {
	 
 		var box = jQuery('#modalBoxes .modalWindow');
 
        //Get the screen height and width
        var maskHeight =jQuery(document).height();
        var maskWidth = jQuery(window).width();
      
        //Set height and width to mask to fill up the whole screen
        jQuery('.cblt-sneezeguard').css({'width':maskWidth,'height':maskHeight, 'top':'0px', 'left':'0px'});
               
        //Get the window height and width
        var winH = jQuery(window).height();
        var winW = jQuery(window).width();

        //Set the popup window to center
        box.css('top',  winH/2 - box.height()/2);
        box.css('left', winW/2 - box.width()/2);
	});	
});

</script>

handler:function(eventName, publisherData, subscriberData) {
function setCookie() {
	var exdate=new Date();
	exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + 365);
	document.cookie="cbltEdmunds=true; expires="+exdate.toUTCString();
}

function getCookie(c_name) {
	var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");
	for (i=0;i<ARRcookies.length;i++) {
		x=ARRcookies[i].substr(0,ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
		y=ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);
		x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
		if (x==c_name) {
			return unescape(y);
		}
	}
}

function runEdmunds() {
	window._edw = {"account":"cblt8275", "data":{}};
	var edw = document.createElement('script'); 
	edw.type = 'text/javascript'; 
	edw.async = true;
	edw.src = 'http://static.ed.edmunds-media.com/edmunds-webassets/current/wro/edw-partner-cblt8275.js';
	var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; 
	s.parentNode.insertBefore(edw, s);
}

function checkEdmunds() {
	var tagged=getCookie("cbltEdmunds");
	if (tagged==null || tagged=="") {
		setCookie();
		runEdmunds();
	}
}

checkEdmunds();
},
source:'Edmunds'
